Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 97, the original release of the Apollo 11 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Luminary 99 revision 1 previously transcribed from a digitized copy of that program. The code was then updated by undoing changes described in original Luminary memos 83 and 85, using asterisks indicating changed lines in the listing as a guide. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152D. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Luminary 099 revision 001 printout, although the added code would likely have changed page numbers for a real Luminary 97 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

020759,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
020760,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
020761,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 97.
020762,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
020763,000006:                                                                                                  ##              original release of the flight software for the Lunar 
020764,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 11.
020765,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Luminary 99
020766,000009:                                                                                                  ##              revision 001, using asterisks indicating changed lines in
020767,000010:                                                                                                  ##              the listing and Luminary Memos #83 and #85, which list 
020768,000011:                                                                                                  ##              changes between Luminary 97 and 98, and 98 and 99. The
020769,000012:                                                                                                  ##              code has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
020770,000013:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Luminary 97 in NASA drawing
020771,000014:                                                                                                  ##              2021152D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
020772,000015:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
020773,000016:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 492-613
020774,000017:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
020775,000018:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
020776,000019:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
020777,000020:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-07-28 MAS  Created from Luminary 99.

020780,000023:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
020781,000024: 
020782,000025:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020783,000026: 
020784,000027:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
020785,000028:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
020786,000029: 
020787,000030:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020788,000031: 
020789,000032:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
020790,000033:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
020791,000034:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
020792,000035:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
020793,000036: 
020794,000037:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020795,000038: 
020796,000039:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
020797,000040: 
020798,000041:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020799,000042: 
020800,000043:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
020801,000044:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
020802,000045:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
020803,000046:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
020804,000047:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
020805,000048:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
020806,000049:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
020807,000050:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
020808,000051:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
020809,000052:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
020810,000053: 
020811,000054:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
020812,000055: 
020813,000056:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
020814,000057:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
020815,000058: 
020816,000059:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
020817,000060: 
020818,000061:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
020819,000062: 
020820,000063:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
020821,000064: 
020822,000065:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
020823,000066: 
020824,000067:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020825,000068: 
020826,000069:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020827,000070: 
020828,000071:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
020829,000072: 
020830,000073:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
020831,000074: 
020832,000075:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
020833,000076: 
020834,000077: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
020835,000078: 
020836,000079: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
020837,000080: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
020838,000081: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
020839,000082: 
020840,000083: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
020841,000084: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

021249,000492:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021250,000493: 
021251,000494:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021252,000495:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021253,000496:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021254,000497: 
021255,000498:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021256,000499: 
021257,000500:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021258,000501:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021259,000502:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021260,000503:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021261,000504: 
021262,000505:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021263,000506:

021265,000508:

021338,000581:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021339,000582:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021340,000583: 
021341,000584:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021342,000585:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021343,000586: 
021344,000587:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021345,000588: 
021346,000589:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021347,000590:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021348,000591: 
021349,000592:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021350,000593: 
021351,000594:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021352,000595:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021353,000596: 
021354,000597:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021355,000598: 
021356,000599:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021357,000600:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021358,000601:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021359,000602: 
021360,000603:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021361,000604: 
021362,000605:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021363,000606:                                                                                                  #        UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
021364,000607:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
021365,000608: 
021366,000609:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021367,000610: 
021368,000611:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM
021369,000612:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
021370,000613: 
021371,000614:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021372,000615: 
021373,000616:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
021374,000617: 
021375,000618:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021376,000619: 
021377,000620:                                                                                                  #        SEE LSR22.1, LSR22.2, LSR22.3
021378,000621: 
021379,000622:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021380,000623: 
021381,000624:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
021382,000625: 
021383,000626:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021384,000627: 
021385,000628:                                                                                                  #        SEE LSR22.1, LSR22.2, LSR22.3
021386,000629: 
021387,000630: 24,2451  E7,1737                                  EBANK=   LRS22.1X

021553,000796:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021554,000797:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021555,000798: 
021556,000799:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021557,000800:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021558,000801: 
021559,000802:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021560,000803: 
021561,000804:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021562,000805:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021563,000806: 
021564,000807:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021565,000808: 
021566,000809:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021567,000810:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021568,000811: 
021569,000812:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021570,000813: 
021571,000814:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021572,000815:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021573,000816:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021574,000817:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021575,000818: 
021576,000819:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021577,000820:                                                                                                  #        
021578,000821:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021579,000822:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021580,000823: 
021581,000824:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021582,000825: 
021583,000826:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021584,000827:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021585,000828:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021586,000829: 
021587,000830:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021588,000831: 
021589,000832:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021590,000833: 
021591,000834:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021592,000835: 
021593,000836:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021594,000837: 
021595,000838:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021596,000839: 
021597,000840:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021598,000841: 
021599,000842:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021600,000843: 
021601,000844:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021602,000845: 
021603,000846: 24,2674  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021604,000847: 24,2674                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
021605,000848: 24,2674           44736        R21LEM             CS       BIT14                                 #  REMOVE RR SELF TRACK ENABLE
021606,000849: 24,2675           00006                           EXTEND

021785,001028:

021862,001105:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
021863,001106:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021864,001107: 
021865,001108:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021866,001109:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021867,001110: 
021868,001111:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021869,001112: 
021870,001113:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
021871,001114:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
021872,001115:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
021873,001116: 
021874,001117:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
021875,001118: 
021876,001119:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
021877,001120:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
021878,001121:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
021879,001122:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
021880,001123: 
021881,001124:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021882,001125: 
021883,001126:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
021884,001127:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
021885,001128:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
021886,001129: 
021887,001130:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021888,001131: 
021889,001132:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
021890,001133:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
021891,001134:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
021892,001135: 
021893,001136:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021894,001137: 
021895,001138:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
021896,001139: 
021897,001140:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
021898,001141: 
021899,001142:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
021900,001143: 
021901,001144:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021902,001145: 
021903,001146:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
021904,001147: 
021905,001148:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021906,001149: 
021907,001150:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
021908,001151: 
021909,001152: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD

021914,001157: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21

021978,001221:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
021979,001222:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021980,001223: 
021981,001224:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO: 3               DATE: 4-11-67
021982,001225:                                                                                                  #        MOD BY: P VOLANTE   SDC
021983,001226: 
021984,001227:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION -
021985,001228: 
021986,001229:                                                                                                  #        TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
021987,001230:                                                                                                  #        TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
021988,001231:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE.
021989,001232: 
021990,001233:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021991,001234: 
021992,001235:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021993,001236:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R61LEM
021994,001237: 
021995,001238:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021996,001239: 
021997,001240:                                                                                                  #        LPS20.1         VECPOINT
021998,001241:                                                                                                  #        KALCMAN3
021999,001242: 
022000,001243:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022001,001244: 
022002,001245:                                                                                                  #        NORMAL RETURN IS TO CALLER + 1
022003,001246: 
022004,001247:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022005,001248: 
022006,001249:                                                                                                  #        TERMINATE P20 + R61 BY BRANCHING TO P20END IF BOTH TRACKFLAG +
022007,001250:                                                                                                  #        RENDEZVOUS FLAG ARE NOT SET.
022008,001251:

022187,001430:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                                                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022188,001431: 
022189,001432:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022190,001433: 
022191,001434:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022192,001435:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022193,001436:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022194,001437:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022195,001438:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022196,001439: 
022197,001440:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022198,001441:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022199,001442:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022200,001443:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022201,001444: 
022202,001445:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022203,001446:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022204,001447:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022205,001448:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022206,001449:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022207,001450: 
022208,001451:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022209,001452: 
022210,001453:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022211,001454:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022212,001455: 
022213,001456:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022214,001457: 
022215,001458:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022216,001459:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022217,001460:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022218,001461: 
022219,001462:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022220,001463: 
022221,001464:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022222,001465: 
022223,001466:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022224,001467: 
022225,001468:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022226,001469:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022227,001470: 
022228,001471:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

022271,001514:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                         . IF EITHER:
022272,001515: 
022273,001516:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022274,001517:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022275,001518:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022276,001519:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022277,001520:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022278,001521:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022279,001522:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022280,001523:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022281,001524:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022282,001525:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022283,001526:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022284,001527:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022285,001528:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022286,001529:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022287,001530:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022288,001531:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022289,001532:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022290,001533:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022291,001534:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022292,001535:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022293,001536: 
022294,001537:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022295,001538: 
022296,001539:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022297,001540: 
022298,001541:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022299,001542: 
022300,001543:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022301,001544: 
022302,001545:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022303,001546: 
022304,001547:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP

022343,001586:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022344,001587: 
022345,001588:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022346,001589: 
022347,001590:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022348,001591:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022349,001592:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022350,001593:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022351,001594:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022352,001595:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022353,001596:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022354,001597:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022355,001598:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022356,001599:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022357,001600:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022358,001601:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022359,001602: 
022360,001603:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022361,001604:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022362,001605:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022363,001606: 
022364,001607:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022365,001608: 
022366,001609:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022367,001610: 
022368,001611:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022369,001612:

022371,001614:                                                                                                  #        
022372,001615:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022373,001616: 
022374,001617:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)

022392,001635:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022393,001636: 
022394,001637:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022395,001638:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022396,001639:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022397,001640:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022398,001641:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022399,001642:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022400,001643:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022401,001644:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022402,001645:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022403,001646:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022404,001647:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022405,001648:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022406,001649:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022407,001650:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022408,001651:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022409,001652:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022410,001653: 
022411,001654:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)

022413,001656:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022414,001657: 
022415,001658:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022416,001659: 
022417,001660:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF

022424,001667:

022468,001711:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022469,001712: 
022470,001713:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022471,001714: 
022472,001715:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022473,001716:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022474,001717:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022475,001718:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022476,001719:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022477,001720:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022478,001721:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022479,001722:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022480,001723:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022481,001724:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022482,001725:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022483,001726:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022484,001727:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022485,001728:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022486,001729:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022487,001730:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022488,001731:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022489,001732:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022490,001733:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022491,001734:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022492,001735:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022493,001736:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022494,001737: 
022495,001738:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022496,001739: 
022497,001740:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022498,001741:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022499,001742: 
022500,001743:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022501,001744: 
022502,001745:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022503,001746: 
022504,001747:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022505,001748:

022507,001750:

022509,001752:

022561,001804:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                         IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022562,001805: 
022563,001806:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022564,001807:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022565,001808:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022566,001809:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022567,001810:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022568,001811:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022569,001812:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022570,001813:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022571,001814:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022572,001815:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022573,001816:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022574,001817:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022575,001818:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022576,001819:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022577,001820:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022578,001821:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022579,001822:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022580,001823:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022581,001824:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022582,001825:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022583,001826: 
022584,001827:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022585,001828: 
022586,001829:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022587,001830:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022588,001831:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022589,001832:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022590,001833: 
022591,001834:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022592,001835: 
022593,001836:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022594,001837:

022658,001901:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022659,001902: 
022660,001903:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022661,001904: 
022662,001905:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022663,001906:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022664,001907:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022665,001908:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022666,001909:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022667,001910:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022668,001911:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022669,001912:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022670,001913:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022671,001914:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022672,001915:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022673,001916:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022674,001917:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022675,001918:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022676,001919: 
022677,001920:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022678,001921:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022679,001922:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022680,001923:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022681,001924:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022682,001925: 
022683,001926:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022684,001927: 
022685,001928:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022686,001929:

022688,001931:

022690,001933:

022751,001994:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
022752,001995: 
022753,001996:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022754,001997: 
022755,001998:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
022756,001999:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
022757,002000:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
022758,002001:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
022759,002002:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
022760,002003:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
022761,002004:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
022762,002005:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
022763,002006:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
022764,002007:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
022765,002008:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
022766,002009:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
022767,002010:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022768,002011: 
022769,002012:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022770,002013:                                                                                                  #

022772,002015:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

022861,002104:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
022862,002105: 
022863,002106:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022864,002107: 
022865,002108:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
022866,002109:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
022867,002110:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
022868,002111:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
022869,002112:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
022870,002113:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
022871,002114:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
022872,002115:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
022873,002116:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
022874,002117:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
022875,002118:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
022876,002119:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
022877,002120:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
022878,002121:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
022879,002122:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
022880,002123:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
022881,002124:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
022882,002125:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
022883,002126:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
022884,002127:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
022885,002128:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
022886,002129:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
022887,002130: 
022888,002131:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022889,002132: 
022890,002133:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
022891,002134:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
022892,002135:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022893,002136:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022894,002137: 
022895,002138:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022896,002139: 
022897,002140:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
022898,002141: 
022899,002142:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022900,002143:

022902,002145:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
022903,002146:

022905,002148:

022951,002194:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
022952,002195: 
022953,002196:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
022954,002197:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
022955,002198:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022956,002199:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
022957,002200:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
022958,002201:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022959,002202:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
022960,002203:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
022961,002204:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
022962,002205:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
022963,002206:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
022964,002207:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
022965,002208:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
022966,002209:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
022967,002210:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
022968,002211:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
022969,002212:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
022970,002213:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
022971,002214:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
022972,002215:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
022973,002216:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022974,002217: 
022975,002218:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022976,002219:
