Page 545 

023124,002367:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023125,002368: 
023126,002369:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023127,002370: 
023128,002371:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023129,002372:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023130,002373:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023131,002374:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023132,002375:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023133,002376:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023134,002377:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023135,002378:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023136,002379:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023137,002380:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023138,002381:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023139,002382:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023140,002383:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023141,002384:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023142,002385:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023143,002386:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023144,002387:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023145,002388:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023146,002389:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023147,002390:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023148,002391:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023149,002392:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023150,002393:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023151,002394:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023152,002395:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023153,002396: 
023154,002397:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023155,002398: 
023156,002399:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023157,002400:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023158,002401:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023159,002402: 
023160,002403:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023161,002404:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023162,002405: 
023163,002406:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023164,002407:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023165,002408: 
023166,002409:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023167,002410: 
023168,002411:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023169,002412:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023170,002413: 
023171,002414:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023172,002415:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023173,002416:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023174,002417: 
023175,002418: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023218,002461: 25,2635           20002        B14+B2             OCT      20002                                 
023219,002462:

Page 547 

023221,002464:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023222,002465: 
023223,002466:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023224,002467: 
023225,002468:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023226,002469:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023227,002470:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023228,002471:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023229,002472:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023230,002473:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023231,002474:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023232,002475:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023233,002476:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023234,002477:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023235,002478:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023236,002479:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023237,002480:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023238,002481:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023239,002482:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023240,002483:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023241,002484:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023242,002485:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023243,002486:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023244,002487:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023245,002488:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023246,002489:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023247,002490:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023248,002491:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023249,002492:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023250,002493:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023251,002494:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023252,002495:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023253,002496:                                                                                                  #        CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023254,002497:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023255,002498:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023256,002499:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023257,002500:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023258,002501:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023259,002502:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023260,002503:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023261,002504:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023262,002505: 
023263,002506:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023264,002507: 
023265,002508:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023266,002509: 
023267,002510:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023268,002511: 
023269,002512:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023270,002513:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023271,002514: 
023272,002515:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023273,002516: 
023274,002517:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 548 

023276,002519: 
023277,002520:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023278,002521: 
023279,002522:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023280,002523: 
023281,002524:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023282,002525: 
023283,002526:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023284,002527: 
023285,002528: 25,2636           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
023286,002529: 25,2637           30036                           DCA      CDUT

023890,003133:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
023891,003134:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
023892,003135: 
023893,003136:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023894,003137:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
023895,003138:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
023896,003139:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
023897,003140: 
023898,003141:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE      CALL
023899,003142:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
023900,003143: 
023901,003144:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023902,003145:                                                                                                  #        LEMPREC, CSMPREC
023903,003146: 
023904,003147:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_  RETURN TO CALLER + 2
023905,003148: 
023906,003149:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_  NONE
023907,003150: 
023908,003151:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023909,003152: 
023910,003153:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
023911,003154:                                                                                                  #        LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
023912,003155:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV
023913,003156:                                                                                                  #        RRNBSW CLEARED
023914,003157: 
023915,003158:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZED ERASEABLE
023916,003159:                                                                                                  #        TDEC1 MUST CONTAIN THE TIME FOR EXTRAPOLATION
023917,003160:                                                                                                  #        SEE ORBITAL INTEGRATION ROUTINE
023918,003161: 
023919,003162:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS_
023920,003163:                                                                                                  #        MPAC DESTROYED BY THIS ROUTINE
023921,003164: 
023922,003165: 23,2314                                           BANK     23                                    
023923,003166: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
023924,003167: 24,2000                                           BANK

Page 565 

023926,003169: 24,3255                                           COUNT*   $$/LPS20                              
023927,003170: 
023928,003171: 24,3255           43020        LPS20.1            STQ      BOFF                                  
023929,003172: 24,3256           01757                                    LS21X                                 
023930,003173: 24,3257           01343                                    LOSCMFLG                              #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS NOT CALLED BY R21
023931,003174: 24,3260           51264                                    LMINT                                 #  SO CALL LEMCONIC TO GET LM STATE
023932,003175: 24,3261           77614                           BON                                            #  IF IN R21 AND ON LUNAR SURFACE
023933,003176: 24,3262           04307                                    SURFFLAG                              #  DON'T CALL LEMCONIC
023934,003177: 24,3263           51274                                    CSMINT                                
023935,003178: 24,3264           77624        LMINT              CALL                                           
023936,003179: 24,3265           27100                                    LEMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE LEM
023937,003180: 24,3266           77775                           VLOAD                                          
023938,003181: 24,3267           00001                                    RATT                                  
023939,003182: 24,3270           26352                           STOVL    LMPOS                                 #  SAVE LM POSITION B-29
023940,003183: 24,3271           00007                                    VATT                                  
023941,003184: 24,3272           16360                           STODL    LMVEL                                 #  SAVE LM VELOCITY B-7
023942,003185: 24,3273           00015                                    TAT                                   
023943,003186: 24,3274           34041        CSMINT             STCALL   TDEC1                                 
023944,003187: 24,3275           27066                                    CSMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE CSM
023945,003188: 24,3276           52375                           VLOAD    VSU                                   #  COMPUTE RELATIVE VELOCITY V(CSM) - V(LM)
023946,003189: 24,3277           00007                                    VATT                                  
023947,003190: 24,3300           02360                                    LMVEL

024023,003266:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024024,003267:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024025,003268:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024026,003269:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024027,003270:

024037,003280:

024039,003282:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)

024243,003486:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024244,003487:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024245,003488:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024246,003489: 
024247,003490:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024248,003491:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024249,003492:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024250,003493:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024251,003494: 
024252,003495:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024253,003496:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024254,003497:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024255,003498:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024256,003499:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024257,003500:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024258,003501:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024259,003502: 
024260,003503:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024261,003504:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024262,003505:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024263,003506: 
024264,003507:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024265,003508:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024266,003509:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024267,003510:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024268,003511:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024269,003512:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024270,003513: 
024271,003514:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024272,003515:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024273,003516:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024274,003517:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024275,003518:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024276,003519:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024277,003520:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024278,003521:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024279,003522:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024280,003523:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024281,003524:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN AOG
024282,003525:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024283,003526:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024284,003527:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024285,003528:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024286,003529: 
024287,003530:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024288,003531:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024289,003532:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

Page 575 

024291,003534:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T

024684,003927: 
024685,003928:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024686,003929:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
024687,003930:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
024688,003931:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024689,003932: 
024690,003933:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024691,003934:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
024692,003935:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
024693,003936: 
024694,003937:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024695,003938:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024696,003939:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR

Page 583 

024698,003941:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
024699,003942:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024700,003943:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024701,003944: 
024702,003945:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024703,003946:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024704,003947:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024705,003948:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024706,003949:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024707,003950:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
024708,003951:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024709,003952:

024814,004057: 
024815,004058:                                                                                                  #  GETULC
024816,004059: 
024817,004060:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE RELATIVE POSITION VECTOR BETWEEN THE CSM

024844,004087:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
024845,004088: 
024846,004089:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY

024908,004151:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
024909,004152:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO 0                      BY P VOLANTE   SDC              DATE 1-15-67
024910,004153: 
024911,004154:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024912,004155: 
024913,004156:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
024914,004157:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
024915,004158:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
024916,004159:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
024917,004160: 
024918,004161:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
024919,004162: 
024920,004163:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024921,004164: 
024922,004165:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM

024924,004167:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
024925,004168:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
024926,004169:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
024927,004170: 
024928,004171:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
024929,004172:

024931,004174:

Page 594 

025163,004406:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025164,004407:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025165,004408: 
025166,004409:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025167,004410: 
025168,004411:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025169,004412:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025170,004413:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025171,004414:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025172,004415:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025173,004416:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025174,004417: 
025175,004418:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025176,004419: 
025177,004420:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025178,004421: 
025179,004422:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025180,004423:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025181,004424:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025182,004425:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025183,004426:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025184,004427:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025185,004428: 
025186,004429:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025187,004430: 
025188,004431:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025189,004432: 
025190,004433:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025191,004434:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025192,004435:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025193,004436:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025194,004437:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 595 

025196,004439: 
025197,004440:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025198,004441: 
025199,004442:                                                                                                  #        NOR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025200,004443:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025201,004444:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025202,004445:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025203,004446: 
025204,004447:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025205,004448: 
025206,004449:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)

Page 600 

025393,004636:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025394,004637: 
025395,004638:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025396,004639:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025397,004640:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025398,004641:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025399,004642:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025400,004643: 
025401,004644:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025402,004645:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025403,004646: 
025404,004647: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025405,004648: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025406,004649: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025407,004650: 
025408,004651: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025409,004652: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025410,004653: 
025411,004654: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025412,004655: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025413,004656: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025414,004657: 
025415,004658: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025416,004659: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025417,004660: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025418,004661: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025419,004662: 
025420,004663: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025421,004664: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025422,004665: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025423,004666: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025424,004667: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025425,004668: 
025426,004669: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025427,004670: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025428,004671: 32,2565           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025429,004672: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025430,004673: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025431,004674: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025432,004675: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025433,004676: 
025434,004677: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025435,004678: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025436,004679: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025437,004680: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025438,004681: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025439,004682: 
025440,004683: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025441,004684: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025442,004685:

Page 601 

025444,004687:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025445,004688: 
025446,004689: 32,2601           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1

025480,004723:                                                                                                  #  THE COSINE IS APPROXIMATELY COS(.5 DEG) OR GREATER (I.E. SMALLER ANGLE).
